[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDuring fuzz testing of the XLIFF parser component, the Jazzer security sanitizer [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdetected a Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m attempt. An HTTP connection to [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m“jazze.com:[0m[1;36m80[0m[39m” was initiated based on untrusted input, triggering a [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`FuzzerSecurityIssueMedium` exception. The sanitizer’s checks in [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ServerSideRequestForgery` prevented the outbound socket connection.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue Overview  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  A fuzzer-provided input caused the XML parsing layer to resolve an external [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentity over HTTP. While processing an XLIFF document via Apache Tika’s [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`XLIFF12Parser` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mthrough the SAX-based XML entity manager[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the code attempted to [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mopen an `HttpURLConnection` to an attacker-controlled destination [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`jazze.com:[0m[1;36m80[0m[39m`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJazzer’s SSRF sanitizer intercepted this call and raised an exception.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The issue is classified as Server Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. Untrusted data [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minfluenced the destination of an outbound network request, creating the risk of [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munauthorized internal access or data exfiltration.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The exception originates in [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.code_intelligence.jazzer.sanitizers.ServerSideRequestForgery.checkSsrf` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m127[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and `checkSsrfSocket` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m71[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The stack trace shows low-level socket connect calls [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`java.net.Socket.connect`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m invoked by `HttpURLConnection` during XML external [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentity resolution [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`XMLEntityManager.setupCurrentEntity`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The parser in question is `org.apache.tika.parser.xliff.XLIFF12Parser`, driven [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mby the harness in `com.example.XliffParserFuzzer`.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code Areas for Investigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  To fully understand the scope of this SSRF issue, review:  [0m                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Any network-accessing utilities or wrappers used by the parser [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., calls to[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe codebase’s XLIFF parser triggered a Jazzer-detected Server-Side Request Forgery[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m when processing untrusted XML: the SAX parser followed an external entity [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreference and opened a socket to jazze.com:[0m[1;36m80[0m[39m. A proposed patch replaced the manual[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`SAXParserFactory` instantiation in XLIFF12Parser with a call to [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.getSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcontext[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, hoping to centralize XML parser creation [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mand its security settings[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. However, the build failed because [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`XMLReaderUtils.getSAXParser` is defined with no parameters, so passing a [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`ParseContext` argument caused a compilation error.[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInitial issue  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- A Jazzer fuzzing run threw a `FuzzerSecurityIssueMedium: Server Side Request [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mForgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` exception: the XML parser in XLIFF12Parser connected to [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mjazze.com:[0m[1;36m80[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The stack trace shows the default JAXP [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mSAXParserFactory.newInstance[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.newSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` invocation, then the parser [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mresolving an external entity via `HttpURLConnection`, culminating in the network [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcall.  [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This represents an SSRF risk: untrusted XML input can cause outbound connections [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto attacker-controlled or internal endpoints.[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mImportant observations  [0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The vulnerable code path is in `[0m[1;35mXLIFF12Parser._parse[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, where a plain [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`SAXParserFactory` is used without any security configuration [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno禁 external [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentities or custom `EntityResolver`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The failure reproduces consistently under the fuzzer’s harness [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`XliffParserFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch attempt  [0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The diff removes the manual factory setup [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines creating `factory`, enabling [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnamespace awareness, catching `ParserConfigurationException`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and replaces it with:[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  `SAXParser parser = [0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.getSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[39mcontext[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;`  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- An import for `org.apache.tika.utils.XMLReaderUtils` is added.  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The goal appears to be delegating parser creation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand security mitigations[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to a[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mshared utility.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPatch result  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- During Maven compile, a single error arises:  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  `method getSAXParser in class XMLReaderUtils cannot be applied to given types; [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mrequired: no arguments, found: ParseContext`  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This indicates `[0m[1;35mXMLReaderUtils.getSAXParser[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` is defined without parameters, so [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe new call signature is invalid. No other compilation errors are reported.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAreas for further investigation  [0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- XMLReaderUtils class: its available overloads, intended usage, and how security [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfeatures [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., disabling external entities[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are configured.  [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ParseContext usage: whether the context must be passed differently or omitted.  [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Other parsers in the codebase [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., HTMLParser, PDFParser[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that rely on [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mXMLReaderUtils—or that still manually configure SAXParserFactory—to unify the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mapproach.  [0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Tests and examples of XMLReaderUtils to verify correct method signatures and [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexpected parameters.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Initial Issue Log[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mHere is the initial issue log of the codebase:[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<issue>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m== Java Exception: com.code_intelligence.jazzer.api.FuzzerSecurityIssueMedium: [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mServer Side Request Forgery [0m[1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
